\"k8s.io/pod-security-admission/api\"\n)\n\n/*\nContainers must be required to run as non-root users.\n\n**Restricted 1.0+\nfunc CheckRunAsNonRoot() Check {\n        return Check{\n                ID:    \"runAsNonRoot\",\n                Level: api.LevelRestricted,\n                Versions: []VersionedCheck{\n                        {\n                                MinimumVersion: api.MajorMinorVersion(1, 0),\n                                CheckPod:       runAsNonRoot_1_0,\n                        },\n                },\n        }\n}\n\nfunc runAsNonRoot_1_0(podMetadata *metav1.ObjectMeta, podSpec *corev1.PodSpec) CheckResult {\n        // See KEP-127: https://github.com/kubernetes/enhancements/blob/308ba8d/keps/sig-node/127-user-namespaces/README.md?plain=1#L411-L447\n        if relaxPolicyForUserNamespacePod(podSpec) {\n                return CheckResult{Allowed: true}\n        }\n\n        // things that explicitly set runAsNonRoot=false\n        var badSetters []string\n\n        podRunAsNonRoot := false\n        if podSpec.SecurityContext != nil && podSpec.SecurityContext.RunAsNonRoot != nil {\n                if !*podSpec.SecurityContext.RunAsNonRoot {\n                        badSetters = append(badSetters, \"pod\")\n                } else {\n                        podRunAsNonRoot = true\n                }\n        }\n\n        // containers that explicitly set runAsNonRoot=false\n        var explicitlyBadContainers []string\n        // containers that didn't set runAsNonRoot and aren't caught by a pod-level runAsNonRoot=true\n        var implicitlyBadContainers []string\n\n        visitContainers(podSpec, func(container *corev1.Container) {\n                if container.SecurityContext != nil && container.SecurityContext.RunAsNonRoot != nil {\n                        // container explicitly set runAsNonRoot\n                        if !*container.SecurityContext.RunAsNonRoot {\n                                // container explicitly set runAsNonRoot to a bad value\n                                explicitlyBadContainers = append(explicitlyBadContainers, container.Name)\n                        }\n                } else {\n                        // container did not explicitly set runAsNonRoot\n                        if !podRunAsNonRoot {\n                                // no pod-level runAsNonRoot=true, so this container implicitly has a bad value\n                                implicitlyBadContainers = append(implicitlyBadContainers, container.Name)\n                        }\n                }\n        })\n\n        if len(explicitlyBadContainers) > 0 {\n                badSetters = append(\n                        badSetters,\n                        fmt.Sprintf(\n                                \"%s %s\",\n                                pluralize(\"container\", \"containers\", len(explicitlyBadContainers)),\n                                joinQuote(explicitlyBadContainers),\n                        ),\n                )\n        }\n       ForbiddenReason: \"runAsNonRoot != true\",\n                        ForbiddenDetail: fmt.Sprintf(\"%s must not set securityContext.runAsNonRoot=false\", strings.Join(badSetters, \" and \")),\n                }\n        }\n\n        // pod didn't set runAsNonRoot and not all containers opted into runAsNonRoot\n        if len(implicitlyBadContainers) > 0 {\n                return CheckResult{\n https://docs.google.com/document/d/1Tjxzjjuy4SQsFSUVXZbvqVb64hjNAG5CQX8bK7Yda9w\n// note: usernames on Windows are NOT case sensitive!\nfunc verifyRunAsNonRoot(pod *v1.Pod, container *v1.Container, return nil.\n        if effectiveSc == nil || effectiveSc.RunAsNonRoot == nil || !*effectiveSc.RunAsNonRoot {\n                return nil\n        }\n        if effectiveSc.RunAsUser != nil {\n                klog.InfoS(\"Windows container does not support SecurityContext.RunAsUser, please use SecurityContext.WindowsOptions\",\n                        \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"containerName\", klog.InfoS(\"Windows container does not support SecurityContext.RunAsGroup\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"containerName\", container.Name)\n        }\n        // Verify that if runAsUserName is set for Core API Validation (pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go)\\n\\nThis file performs API-server-side structural validation:\\n- `ValidateSecurityContext()`: Validates container-level security context including `privileged` (checks against cluster policy via `capabilities.Get().AllowPrivileged`), `seccompProfile` (via `validateSeccompProfileField`), and `capabilities` (checks CAP_SYS_ADMIN with allowPrivilegeEscalation=false).\\n- `validatePodSpecSecurityContext()`: Validates pod-level security context including `seccompProfile`.\\n- `validateSeccompProfileField()`: Validates the structure of a SeccompProfile field.\\n- `ValidateSeccompProfile()`: Validates legacy annotation-based seccomp profile strings.\\n- `ValidateSeccompPodAnnotations()`: Validates seccomp annotations on pods.\\n- `validateSeccompProfileType()`: Validates SeccompProfileType enum values.\\n- `validateSeccompAnnotationsAndFields()` / `validateSeccompAnnotationsAndFieldsMatch()`: Ensures consistency between seccomp annotations and field-based seccomp profiles.\\n\\n## 3. Kubelet Runtime Enforcement (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/)\\n\\nThese files enforce security context at container start time:\\n\\n### runAsNonRoot enforcement\\n- **security_context_others.go** (Linux): `verifyRunAsNonRoot()` checks that if `runAsNonRoot=true`, the container's effective UID is not 0.\\n- **security_context_windows.go** (Windows): `verifyRunAsNonRoot()` checks that the effective username is not 'ContainerAdministrator'.\\n- **kuberuntime_container.go**: Calls `verifyRunAsNonRoot()` in `generateContainerConfig()`.\\n\\n### Privileged container check\\n- **kuberuntime_sandbox.go**: `generatePodSandboxLinuxConfig()` uses `HasPrivilegedContainer()` to set the sandbox's privileged flag.\\n- **security_context.go**: `convertToRuntimeSecurityContext()` passes `Privileged` to the runtime API.\\n\\n### Capabilities\\n- **security_context.go**: `convertToRuntimeCapabilities()` converts v1.Capabilities to runtime API capabilities.\\n\\n### seccompProfile enforcement\\n- **helpers.go**: `fieldSeccompProfile()` resolves a SeccompProfile field to a runtime SecurityProfile; `getSeccompProfile()` selects the effective seccomp profile (container-level overrides pod-level).\\n- **security_context.go**: `determineEffectiveSecurityContext()` calls `getSeccompProfile()` to set the synthesized seccomp profile.\\n\\n## 4. Security Context Utilities (pkg/securitycontext/)\\n\\n- **util.go**: `DetermineEffectiveSecurityContext()` merges pod-level and container-level security contexts (including RunAsNonRoot, Privileged, Capabilities); `securityContextFromPodSecurityContext()` synthesizes a container SecurityContext from pod-level settings.\\n- **accessors.go**: Defines `PodSecurityContextAccessor`, `ContainerSecurityContextAccessor` interfaces and their implementations, providing typed access to RunAsNonRoot, SeccompProfile, Capabilities, and Privileged fields.\\n\\n## 5. Container Helpers (pkg/kubelet/container/helpers.go)\\n\\n- `HasPrivilegedContainer()`: Checks if any container in a pod has `securityContext.privileged=true`.\"\n}\n",

Eventually they may be per-user\ntype Capabilities struct {\n        AllowPrivileged bool\n\n        // Pod sources from which to allow privileged capabilities like host networking, sharing the host\n        // IPC namespace, and sharing the host PID namespace.\n        PrivilegedSources PrivilegedSources\n\n        // PerConnectionBandwidthLimitBytesPerSec limits the throughput of each connection (currently only used for proxy, exec, attach)\n        PerConnectionBandwidthLimitBytesPerSec int64\n}\n\n// PrivilegedSources defines the pod sources allowed to make privileged requests for certain types\n// of capabilities like host networking, sharing the host IPC namespace, and sharing the host PID namespace.\ntype PrivilegedSources struct {\n        // List of pod sources for which using host network is allowed.\n        HostNetworkSources []string\n\n        // List of pod sources for which using host pid namespace is allowed.\n        HostPIDSources []string\n\n        // List of pod sources for which using host ipc is allowed.\n        HostIPCSources []string\n}\n\nvar capInstance struct {\n        once         sync.Once\n        lock         sync.Mutex\n        capabilities *Capabilities\n}\n\n// Initialize the capability set.  This can only be done once per binary, subsequent calls are ignored.\nfunc Initialize(c Capabilities) {\n        // Only do this once\n        capInstance.once.Do(func() {\n                capInstance.capabilities = &c\n        })\n}\n\n// Setup the capability set.  It wraps Initialize for improving usability.\nfunc Setup(allowPrivileged bool, perConnectionBytesPerSec int64) {\n        Initialize(Capabilities{\n                AllowPrivileged:                        allowPrivileged,\n                PerConnectionBandwidthLimitBytesPerSec: perConnectionBytesPerSec,\n        })\n}\n\n// ResetForTest resets the capabilities to a given state for testing purposes.\n// This function should only be called from tests.\nfunc ResetForTest() {\n        capInstance.lock.Lock()\n        defer capInstance.lock.Unlock()\n        capInstance.capabilities = nil\n        capInstance.once = sync.Once{}\n}\n\n// Get returns a read-only copy of the system capabilities.\nfunc Get() Capabilities {\n        capInstance.lock.Lock()\n        defer capInstance.lock.Unlock()\n        // This check prevents clobbering of capabilities that might've been set via SetForTests\n        if capInstance.capabilities == nil {\n                Initialize(Capabilities{\n                        AllowPrivileged: false,\n                        PrivilegedSources: PrivilegedSources{\n                                HostNetworkSources: []string{},\n                                HostPIDSources:     []string{},\n                                HostIPCSources:     []string{},\n                        },\n                })\n        }\n        return *capInstance.capabilities\n}"
